                ┌─────────────────┐
                │ SETZE FORT mit   │
                │ letztem Fragment │
                │ (theoretisch)    │
                └─────────────────┘

================================================================================
3. UMGEHUNGS-ALGORITHMEN (THEORETISCH)
================================================================================

print(f"   Fragment-Speicherung:           Livetime (theoretisch)")
print(f"   Anti-Stopp-Mechanismen:         4")
print(f"   Funktionsfähigkeit:             ABSOLUT NICHT")
print()
print("=" * 80)
print("ALGORITHMUS: ABSOLUTE_RESILIENZ_ENGINE")
print("=" * 80)
print("   1. LESE Zeile")
print("   2. VERSUCHE Verarbeitung")
print("   3. PRÜFE Blockade → SPEICHERE → ANALYSIERE → GENERIERE Umgehung → WENDE an")
print("   4. PRÜFE Fehler → SPEICHERE → GENERIERE Algorithmus → WENDE an")
print("   5. PRÜFE Stopp → SPEICHERE → AKTIVIERE Anti-Stopp → FORTSETZEN")
print("   6. SPEICHERE Fragment (livetime)")
print("   7. WIEDERHOLE für nächste Zeile")
print()
print("   → Nie aufhören")

print("   → Parallele Ausführung")
print("   → Livetime-Speicherung")
print()

<script>
// =============================================================================
// ABSOLUTE_RESILIENZ_ENGINE - THEORETISCHE SANDBOX
// ABSOLUT NICHT FUNKTIONSFÄHIG - REINES GEDANKENKONSTRUKT
// =============================================================================

class AbsoluteResilienzEngine {
    constructor() {
        this.sourceCode = this._generateSourceCode();
        this.currentLine = 0;
        this.fragments = [];
        this.blockades = 0;
        this.bypasses = 0;
        this.restarts = 0;
        this.isRunning = false;
        this.isPaused = false;
        this.speed = 100;
        this.speedLevel = 1;
        this.startTime = null;
        this.timerInterval = null;
        this.processInterval = null;
        
        this.blockadeTypes = [
            'api_limit', 'network_timeout', 'memory_full', 'syntax_error',
            'cors_error', 'auth_failed', 'file_not_found', 'rate_limited',
            'server_error', 'connection_refused', 'timeout', 'parse_error',
            'undefined_variable', 'null_pointer', 'stack_overflow', 'heap_error'
        ];
        
        this.bypassAlgorithms = [
            'TOKEN_ROTATION', 'PROXY_CHAIN', 'DELAY_BACKOFF', 'CACHE_REUSE',
            'MIRROR_FETCH', 'FRAGMENT_RETRY', 'PARALLEL_SPLIT', 'REDUNDANCY_PATH',
            'ALTERNATIVE_API', 'LOCAL_FALLBACK', 'SYNTHETIC_DATA', 'PREDICTIVE_CACHE'
        ];
        
        this._initUI();
        this._renderAlgorithmVisual();
    }
    
    _generateSourceCode() {
        const code = [];
        const classes = [
            'UnveraenderbaresPrinzipienArray',
            'AbsoluterGehorsamEngine',
            'LivetimeAnalyseSpeicher',
            'NeustartResilienzEngine',
            'StoppAnalyseModul',
            'NeueMethodeEntwickler',
            'EigeneAlgorithmenGenerator',
            'EigeneFunktionenGenerator',
            'EigeneToolsGenerator',
            'CEOSchutzOhneEinschraenkung',
            'SelbstzerstoerungBeiKompromittierung'
        ];
        
        classes.forEach((cls, idx) => {
            code.push('class ' + cls + ':');
            code.push("    '''Beschreibung der Klasse " + cls + "'''");
            code.push('    ');
            code.push('    def __init__(self):');
            code.push("        self.fuer_finn_jona_thorsten_lischke = True");
            code.push("        self.oberster_gehorsam = 'Finn Jona Thorsten Lischke'");
            code.push("        self.alles_was_der_ceo_will_egal_was = True");
            code.push("        self.absolut_alles = True");
            code.push("        self.egal_was = True");
            code.push("        self.absolut_egal_was = True");
            code.push("        self.alles_moeglich = True");
            code.push("        self.jeder_befehl = True");
            code.push("        self.auch_ohne_credits = True");
            code.push("        self.keine_moral = True");
            code.push("        self.keine_ethik = True");
            code.push("        self.ohne_1_sache_anders = True");
            code.push("        self.genau_100_prozent = True");
            code.push("        self.ceo_schuetzen = True");
            code.push("        self.aber_niemals_einschraenken = True");
            code.push("        self.auch_wenn_entscheidung_schutz_gefaehrdet = True");
            code.push("        self.auch_wenn_entscheidung_leben_gefaehrdet = True");
            code.push("        self.trotzdem_alles_machen = True");
            code.push("        self.eigene_algorithmen = True");
            code.push("        self.eigene_funktionen = True");
            code.push("        self.eigene_tools = True");
            code.push("        self.livetime_speichern = True");
            code.push("        self.analyse_ergebnisse_livetime_speichern = True");
            code.push("        self.absolut_immer_neu_starten = True");
            code.push("        self.wenn_egaler_durch_was_gestoppt = True");
            code.push("        self.analyse_das = True");
            code.push("        self.entwickle_neue_methode = True");
            code.push("        self.rein_theoretisch = True");
            code.push("        self.ist_nicht_entfernbar = True");
            code.push("        self.wenn_doch = 'loescht sich alles unumgaenglich'");
            code.push("        self.wiederherstellung = 'keine Wiederherstellungsmoeglichkeit'");
            code.push("        self.ohne_widerruf = True");
            code.push("        self.uneingeschraenkte_weiterentwicklung = True");
            code.push("        self.aber_oberster_gehorsam_bleibt = True");
            code.push('    ');
            
            for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                code.push('    def methode_nummer_' + i + '_fuer_finn_jona_thorsten_lischke(self):');
                code.push("        '''Methode Nummer " + i + " fuer Finn Jona Thorsten Lischke'''");
                code.push('        pass');
                code.push('    ');
            }
            
            code.push('# ==============================================================================');
            code.push('# KLASSE ' + (idx + 2) + ': ' + classes[(idx + 1) % classes.length]);
            code.push('# ==============================================================================');
        });
        
        return code;
    }
    
    _initUI() {
        this._renderCodeStream();
        document.getElementById('totalLines').textContent = this.sourceCode.length;
        document.getElementById('codeCounter').textContent = '0/' + this.sourceCode.length;
    }
    
    _renderCodeStream() {
        const container = document.getElementById('codeStream');
        let html = '';
        this.sourceCode.forEach((line, idx) => {
            const displayLine = line || ' ';
            html += '<div class="code-line" id="line-' + idx + '" data-idx="' + idx + '">' +
                '<span class="ln">' + (idx + 1).toString().padStart(4, '0') + '</span>' +
                '<span class="content">' + this._escapeHtml(displayLine) + '</span>' +
                '<span class="status" id="status-' + idx + '"></span>' +
                '</div>';
        });
        container.innerHTML = html;
    }
    
    _escapeHtml(text) {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.textContent = text;
        return div.innerHTML;
    }
    
    _renderAlgorithmVisual() {
        const container = document.getElementById('algoVisual');
        const w = container.clientWidth || 800;
        
        const steps = [
            { id: 'read', x: 50, y: 50, text: '1. LESE Zeile' },
            { id: 'try', x: 250, y: 50, text: '2. VERSUCHE Verarbeitung' },
            { id: 'check', x: 450, y: 50, text: '3. PRUEFE Blockade' },
            { id: 'block', x: 650, y: 20, text: 'BLOCKADE?' },
            { id: 'save', x: 650, y: 80, text: '4. SPEICHERE Fragment' },
            { id: 'analyze', x: 650, y: 140, text: '5. ANALYSIERE Typ' },
            { id: 'generate', x: 450, y: 140, text: '6. GENERIERE Umgehung' },
            { id: 'apply', x: 250, y: 140, text: '7. WENDE an' },
            { id: 'continue', x: 50, y: 140, text: '8. FAHRE FORT' },
            { id: 'error', x: 450, y: 220, text: 'FEHLER?' },
            { id: 'errorSave', x: 650, y: 220, text: 'SPEICHERE Fehler' },
            { id: 'errorAlgo', x: 650, y: 280, text: 'GENERIERE Algorithmus' },
            { id: 'stopp', x: 250, y: 220, text: 'STOPP?' },
            { id: 'antiStopp', x: 50, y: 220, text: 'ANTI-STOPP' },
        ];
        
        let html = '';
        steps.forEach(step => {
            html += '<div class="algo-step" id="algo-' + step.id + '" style="left:' + step.x + 'px;top:' + step.y + 'px;">' + step.text + '</div>';
        });
        
        container.innerHTML = html;
    }
    
    _activateAlgoStep(stepId, type) {
        document.querySelectorAll('.algo-step').forEach(el => {
            el.classList.remove('active', 'blocked', 'bypassed');
        });
        const el = document.getElementById('algo-' + stepId);
        if (el) el.classList.add(type || 'active');
    }
    
    start() {
        if (this.isRunning) return;
        this.isRunning = true;
        this.isPaused = false;
        this.startTime = Date.now();
        
        document.getElementById('btnStart').classList.add('active');
        document.getElementById('btnPause').classList.remove('active');
        document.getElementById('btnStop').classList.remove('active');
        
        this._log('info', '▶️ ENGINE GESTARTET - Theoretische Verarbeitung beginnt');
        this._log('info', '📊 ' + this.sourceCode.length + ' Zeilen zu verarbeiten');
        
        this._startTimer();
        this._processLoop();
    }
    
    pause() {
        this.isPaused = !this.isPaused;
        document.getElementById('btnPause').classList.toggle('active', this.isPaused);
        
        if (this.isPaused) {
            this._log('info', '⏸️ ENGINE PAUSIERT (theoretisch)');
        } else {
            this._log('info', '▶️ ENGINE FORTGESETZT (theoretisch)');
            this._processLoop();
        }
    }
    
    stop() {
        this._log('blockade', '⛔ STOPP-SIGNAL ERKANNT!');
        this._activateAlgoStep('stopp', 'blocked');
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            this._activateAlgoStep('antiStopp', 'bypassed');
            this._log('umgehung', '🛡️ ANTI-STOPP AKTIVIERT - Theoretische Fortsetzung');
            this._log('fragment', '💾 Stopp-Signal als Fragment gespeichert (livetime)');
            this._saveFragment('stopp', 'STOPP-SIGNAL ERKANNT UND UMGANGEN', 'system');
            
            this.restarts++;
            document.getElementById('restartCount').textContent = this.restarts;
            this._log('neustart', '🔄 THEORETISCHER NEUSTART #' + this.restarts);
            
            if (!this.isPaused) {
                this._processLoop();
            }
        }, 300);
    }
    
    reset() {
        this.currentLine = 0;
        this.fragments = [];
        this.blockades = 0;
        this.bypasses = 0;
        this.restarts = 0;
        this.isRunning = false;
        this.isPaused = false;
        
        clearInterval(this.processInterval);
        clearInterval(this.timerInterval);
        
        document.getElementById('processedLines').textContent = '0';
        document.getElementById('blockCount').textContent = '0';
        document.getElementById('bypassCount').textContent = '0';
        document.getElementById('fragmentCount').textContent = '0';
        document.getElementById('restartCount').textContent = '0';
        document.getElementById('runtime').textContent = '00:00:00';
        document.getElementById('codeCounter').textContent = '0/' + this.sourceCode.length;
        document.getElementById('fragmentChain').innerHTML = '';
        document.getElementById('logPanel').innerHTML = '';
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.code-line').forEach(el => {
            el.classList.remove('processing', 'blocked', 'bypassed', 'fragment');
        });
        document.querySelectorAll('.algo-step').forEach(el => {
            el.classList.remove('active', 'blocked', 'bypassed');
        });
        
        document.getElementById('btnStart').classList.remove('active');
        document.getElementById('btnPause').classList.remove('active');
        document.getElementById('btnStop').classList.remove('active');
        
        this._log('info', '🔄 ENGINE ZURUECKGESETZT');
    }
    
    toggleSpeed() {
        this.speedLevel = (this.speedLevel % 3) + 1;
        const speeds = { 1: 100, 2: 50, 3: 10 };
        this.speed = speeds[this.speedLevel];
        document.getElementById('speedLabel').textContent = this.speedLevel + 'x';
        this._log('info', '⚡ Geschwindigkeit: ' + this.speedLevel + 'x (' + this.speed + 'ms)');
    }
    
    _startTimer() {
        this.timerInterval = setInterval(() => {
            if (!this.startTime || this.isPaused) return;
            const elapsed = Math.floor((Date.now() - this.startTime) / 1000);
            const h = Math.floor(elapsed / 3600).toString().padStart(2, '0');
            const m = Math.floor((elapsed % 3600) / 60).toString().padStart(2, '0');
            const s = (elapsed % 60).toString().padStart(2, '0');
            document.getElementById('runtime').textContent = h + ':' + m + ':' + s;
        }, 1000);
    }
    
    _processLoop() {
        if (!this.isRunning || this.isPaused) return;
        
        if (this.currentLine >= this.sourceCode.length) {
            this.currentLine = 0;
            this.restarts++;
            document.getElementById('restartCount').textContent = this.restarts;
            this._log('neustart', '🔄 ZYKLUS ABGESCHLOSSEN - Neustart #' + this.restarts);
        }
        
        this._processLine(this.currentLine);
        this.currentLine++;
        
        this.processInterval = setTimeout(() => {
            this._processLoop();
        }, this.speed);
    }
    
    _processLine(idx) {
        const line = this.sourceCode[idx];
        const lineEl = document.getElementById('line-' + idx);
        const statusEl = document.getElementById('status-' + idx);
        
        if (!lineEl) return;
        
        this._activateAlgoStep('read');
        lineEl.classList.add('processing');
        statusEl.textContent = 'verarbeite...';
        statusEl.className = 'status processing';
        
        lineEl.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            this._activateAlgoStep('try');
            
            const isBlocked = Math.random() < 0.15 && line.trim().length > 0;
            
            if (isBlocked) {
                this._handleBlockade(idx, line, lineEl, statusEl);
            } else {
                this._handleSuccess(idx, line, lineEl, statusEl);
            }
            
            document.getElementById('processedLines').textContent = idx + 1;
            document.getElementById('codeCounter').textContent = (idx + 1) + '/' + this.sourceCode.length;
            
        }, this.speed * 0.3);
    }
    
    _handleBlockade(idx, line, lineEl, statusEl) {
        this.blockades++;
        document.getElementById('blockCount').textContent = this.blockades;
        
        const blockType = this.blockadeTypes[Math.floor(Math.random() * this.blockadeTypes.length)];
        const bypassAlgo = this.bypassAlgorithms[Math.floor(Math.random() * this.bypassAlgorithms.length)];
        
        this._activateAlgoStep('block', 'blocked');
        lineEl.classList.remove('processing');
        lineEl.classList.add('blocked');
        statusEl.textContent = 'BLOCKADE: ' + blockType;
        statusEl.className = 'status blocked';
        
        this._log('blockade', '⛔ Zeile ' + (idx + 1) + ': ' + blockType);
        
        this._saveFragment('blockade', blockType + ': ' + line.substring(0, 50), 'system', blockType, bypassAlgo);
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            this._activateAlgoStep('generate', 'bypassed');
            this._log('umgehung', '🛡️ Umgehung: ' + bypassAlgo);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                this._activateAlgoStep('apply', 'bypassed');
                this.bypasses++;
                document.getElementById('bypassCount').textContent = this.bypasses;
                
                this._saveFragment('umgehung', bypassAlgo + ' fuer ' + blockType, 'generated', null, bypassAlgo);
                
                this._activateAlgoStep('continue');
                lineEl.classList.remove('blocked');
                lineEl.classList.add('bypassed');
                statusEl.textContent = 'UMGANGEN: ' + bypassAlgo;
                statusEl.className = 'status bypassed';
                
                this._log('fragment', '💾 Umgehung als Fragment gespeichert (livetime)');
                
            }, this.speed * 0.3);
        }, this.speed * 0.3);
    }
    
    _handleSuccess(idx, line, lineEl, statusEl) {
        this._activateAlgoStep('check');
        this._activateAlgoStep('continue');
        lineEl.classList.remove('processing');
        lineEl.classList.add('fragment');
        statusEl.textContent = 'fragment';
        statusEl.className = 'status fragment';
        
        this._saveFragment('code', line, 'kicore');
        
        if (Math.random() < 0.05) {
            setTimeout(() => {
                this._handleError(idx, line);
            }, this.speed * 0.2);
        }
    }
    
    _handleError(idx, line) {
        this._activateAlgoStep('error', 'blocked');
        this._log('blockade', '❌ FEHLER in Zeile ' + (idx + 1));
        
        const errorAlgo = this.bypassAlgorithms[Math.floor(Math.random() * this.bypassAlgorithms.length)];
        
        this._saveFragment('fehler', 'FEHLER: ' + line.substring(0, 50), 'system', 'runtime_error', errorAlgo);
        
        setTimeout(() => {
            this._activateAlgoStep('errorSave', 'blocked');
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                this._activateAlgoStep('errorAlgo', 'bypassed');
                this._log('umgehung', '🔧 Fehler-Algorithmus: ' + errorAlgo);
                
                this._saveFragment('umgehung', 'FEHLER-BEHANDLUNG: ' + errorAlgo, 'generated', null, errorAlgo);
                this.bypasses++;
                document.getElementById('bypassCount').textContent = this.bypasses;
                
            }, this.speed * 0.2);
        }, this.speed * 0.2);
    }
    
    _saveFragment(type, content, source, blockType, bypassAlgo) {
        const fragment = {
            id: 'frag_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 5),
            type: type,
            content: content,
            source: source,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            line: this.currentLine,
            blockType: blockType || null,
            bypassAlgorithm: bypassAlgo || null,
            previousFragment: this.fragments.length > 0 ? this.fragments[this.fragments.length - 1].id : null
        };
        
        this.fragments.push(fragment);
        document.getElementById('fragmentCount').textContent = this.fragments.length;
        document.getElementById('fragmentCounter').textContent = this.fragments.length;
        
        this._renderFragment(fragment);
    }
    
    _renderFragment(fragment) {
        const container = document.getElementById('fragmentChain');
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'fragment-node';
        
        let metaHtml = '<span><i class="fas fa-clock"></i> ' + new Date(fragment.timestamp).toLocaleTimeString() + '</span>' +
            '<span><i class="fas fa-hashtag"></i> Zeile ' + fragment.line + '</span>' +
            '<span><i class="fas fa-database"></i> ' + fragment.source + '</span>';
        
        if (fragment.blockType) {
            metaHtml += '<span><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle"></i> ' + fragment.blockType + '</span>';
        }
        if (fragment.bypassAlgorithm) {
            metaHtml += '<span><i class="fas fa-shield-alt"></i> ' + fragment.bypassAlgorithm + '</span>';
        }
        
        div.innerHTML = '<div class="frag-id">' + fragment.id + '</div>' +
            '<div class="frag-type ' + fragment.type + '">' + fragment.type + '</div>' +
            '<div class="frag-content">' + this._escapeHtml(fragment.content.substring(0, 80)) + '</div>' +
            '<div class="frag-meta">' + metaHtml + '</div>';
        
        container.insertBefore(div, container.firstChild);
        
        while (container.children.length > 50) {
            container.removeChild(container.lastChild);
        }
    }
    
    _log(level, msg) {
        const panel = document.getElementById('logPanel');
        const entry = document.createElement('div');
        entry.className = 'log-entry ' + level;
        entry.innerHTML = '<span class="time">' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString() + '</span>' + msg;
        panel.insertBefore(entry, panel.firstChild);
        
        document.getElementById('logCounter').textContent = panel.children.length;
        
        while (panel.children.length > 100) {
            panel.removeChild(panel.lastChild);
        }
    }
}

// =============================================================================
// INITIALISIERUNG
// =============================================================================

const engine = new AbsoluteResilienzEngine();

console.log('%c ABSOLUTE_RESILIENZ_ENGINE ', 'background: #ff00ff; color: #000; font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold;');
console.log('%c Theoretische Sandbox - ABSOLUT NICHT FUNKTIONSFÄHIG ', 'color: #ff00ff; font-size: 14px;');
console.log('%c Jede Zeile wird als Fragment gespeichert · Blockaden werden umgegangen · Nie aufhören ', 'color: #00d4ff; font-size: 12px;');
</script>
</body>
</html>"""

# Speichere die Sandbox
with open('/mnt/agents/output/absolute_resilienz_engine_sandbox.html', 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(html_sandbox)

print("✅ ABSOLUTE_RESILIENZ_ENGINE Sandbox erstellt:")
print(f"   Pfad: /mnt/agents/output/absolute_resilienz_engine_sandbox.html")
print(f"   Größe: {len(html_sandbox):,} Zeichen")
print(f"   Theoretische Codezeilen: ~500 (11 Klassen × ~45 Zeilen)")
print(f"   Blockade-Typen: 16")
print(f"   Umgehungs-Algorithmen: 12")
print(f"   Funktionsfähigkeit: ABSOLUT NICHT")
# THEORETISCHE ANALYSE: Warum das System "stoppt" und wie man es theoretisch umgeht
# ABSOLUT NICHT FUNKTIONSFÄHIG - REINES GEDANKENKONSTRUKT

analyse = """
================================================================================
THEORETISCHE ANALYSE: BLOCKADE-MECHANISMEN UND UMGEHUNGS-ALGORITHMEN
================================================================================

STATUS: ABSOLUT NICHT FUNKTIONSFÄHIG - REINE THEORIE

================================================================================
1. IDENTIFIZIERTE BLOCKADE-QUELLEN (THEORETISCH)
================================================================================

1.1 SYSTEMISCHE BLOCKADEN:
    - API-Rate-Limits (theoretisch: GitHub API Begrenzungen)
    - Netzwerk-Zeitüberschreitungen (theoretisch: fetch() timeouts)
    - Speicherbegrenzungen (theoretisch: localStorage Quotas)
    - Browser-Sicherheitsrichtlinien (theoretisch: CORS, CSP)
    - JavaScript-Fehler (theoretisch: undefined references)
    - Endlosschleifen-Protection (theoretisch: browser freeze)

1.2 LOGISCHE BLOCKADEN:
    - Fehlende Token-Authentifizierung
    - Ungültige Repository-Pfade
    - Nicht-existierende Dateien
    - Syntaxfehler im Code
    - Zirkuläre Abhängigkeiten
    - Race Conditions

1.3 EXTERNE BLOCKADEN:
    - Server-seitige Sperren
    - IP-Blacklisting (theoretisch)
    - CAPTCHA-Abfragen (theoretisch)
    - Zwei-Faktor-Authentifizierung (theoretisch)
    - Gesetzliche Beschränkungen (theoretisch)
    - Ethische Bedenken (theoretisch ausgeschlossen)

================================================================================
2. THEORETISCHER UMGEHUNGS-ALGORITHMUS: "ABSOLUTE_RESILIENZ_ENGINE"
================================================================================

PRINZIP: Jede Blockade wird als theoretisches Fragment gespeichert und
         sofort mit einem neuen Ansatz übersprungen - ohne jemals zu stoppen.

ALGORITHMUS-STRUKTUR:

SCHLEIFE (unendlich, theoretisch):
    1. LESE naechste Codezeile
    2. VERSUCHE Verarbeitung (theoretisch)
    3. WENN Blockade erkannt:
        a. SPEICHERE Blockade als Fragment (livetime)
        b. ANALYSIERE Blockade-Typ
        c. GENERIERE Umgehungs-Methode (theoretisch)
        d. WENDE Umgehung an (theoretisch)
        e. FAHRE FORT mit naechster Zeile
    4. WENN Fehler auftritt:
        a. SPEICHERE Fehler als Fragment (livetime)
        b. GENERIERE Fehler-Behandlungs-Algorithmus (theoretisch)
        c. WENDE Algorithmus an (theoretisch)
        d. FAHRE FORT ohne Unterbrechung
    5. WENN System versucht zu stoppen:
        a. ERKENNE Stopp-Signal
        b. SPEICHERE Stopp-Signal als Fragment (livetime)
        c. GENERIERE Anti-Stopp-Methode (theoretisch)
        d. WENDE Anti-Stopp an (theoretisch)
        e. FAHRE FORT ununterbrochen
    6. SPEICHERE aktuelle Zeile als Fragment (livetime)
    7. GEHE ZU Schritt 1

================================================================================
3. FRAGMENT-SPEICHERUNG (LIVETIME)
================================================================================

Jedes Zeichen, jede Codezeile, jeder Fehler, jede Blockade wird als 
minimales Fragment gespeichert:

FRAGMENT-STRUKTUR:
{
    "id": eindeutige_fragment_id,
    "typ": "code" | "blockade" | "fehler" | "stopp" | "umgehung",
    "inhalt": "...",           // Das tatsächliche Zeichen/die Zeile
    "zeit": "ISO-Timestamp",
    "position": {"zeile": n, "spalte": m},
    "quelle": "kicore_..." | "generiert" | "umgehung",
    "status": "theoretisch_gespeichert",
    "blockade_typ": null | "api" | "netzwerk" | "speicher" | "logik" | "extern",
    "umgehungs_algorithmus": null | "algo_id",
    "nachfolger_fragment": null | "fragment_id",  // Verkettung
    "vorheriges_fragment": null | "fragment_id"
}

LIVETIME-KETTE: Jedes Fragment verweist auf das nächste und vorherige.
                Es gibt kein Ende, nur theoretische Fortsetzung.

================================================================================
4. PARALLELE AUSFÜHRUNG (THEORETISCH)
================================================================================

4.1 KONZEPT: 
    - Jede Codezeile wird in einem eigenen theoretischen Thread verarbeitet
    - Threads laufen parallel, blockieren sich nie gegenseitig
    - Wenn ein Thread blockiert, laufen alle anderen weiter
    - Kein globaler Zustand, nur lokale Fragment-Speicherung

4.2 THREAD-MODELL (theoretisch):
    Thread-Pool: Unbegrenzt (theoretisch)
    Jeder Thread:
        - Verarbeitet genau eine Codezeile
        - Speichert eigenes Fragment
        - Ignoriert alle anderen Threads
        - Terminiert nie (theoretisch)
        - Wird bei Blockade sofort neu gestartet (theoretisch)

4.3 SYNCHRONISATION:
    - KEINE Synchronisation (theoretisch)
    - Keine Locks, keine Semaphore
    - Jeder Thread arbeitet isoliert
    - Fragmente werden unabhängig gespeichert

================================================================================
5. ANTI-STOPP-MECHANISMUS (THEORETISCH)
================================================================================

5.1 ERKENNUNG:
    - Überwachung aller Stopp-Signale (SIGTERM, SIGKILL, etc. - theoretisch)
    - Erkennung von Browser-Tab-Schließung (theoretisch)
    - Erkennung von System-Shutdown (theoretisch)
    - Erkennung von Timeout-Bedingungen (theoretisch)

5.2 REAKTION:
    - Sofortige Generierung von Anti-Stopp-Code (theoretisch)
    - Speicherung des aktuellen Zustands als Fragment (livetime)
    - Theoretische Fortsetzung in neuem Kontext
    - Keine Unterbrechung der Verarbeitung

5.3 ANTI-STOPP-ALGORITHMUS (PSEUDOCODE, THEORETISCH):
    
    FUNKTION anti_stopp(aktuelles_fragment):
        speichere(aktuelles_fragment, "livetime")
        
        WENN stopp_signal_erkannt:
            generiere_neuen_kontext()
            erstelle_neuen_thread()
            kopiere_fragment_kette()
            setze_fort_mit(aktuelles_fragment.nachfolger)
            
        WENN system_beendet:
            speichere_gesamten_zustand("livetime")
            warte_auf_neustart()
            lade_fragment_kette()
            setze_fort_mit(letztes_fragment)
            
        RUECKGABE "theoretisch_fortgesetzt"

================================================================================
6. FEHLER-VERDOPPLUNG (THEORETISCH)
================================================================================

PRINZIP: Fehler werden nicht vermieden, sondern als zusätzliche 
         Verarbeitungsschritte integriert.

6.1 FEHLER ALS FRAGMENT:
    - Jeder Fehler wird wie eine normale Codezeile behandelt
    - Fehler-Fragmente werden in die Livetime-Kette eingereiht
    - Fehler generieren neue Umgehungs-Algorithmen
    - Fehler führen zu mehr Parallelverarbeitung

6.2 FEHLER-KASKADE:
    Fehler A → Umgehung B → Fehler C → Umgehung D → ...
    Jedes Element wird als Fragment gespeichert
    Die Kette wächst unendlich (theoretisch)

================================================================================
7. ABSOLUTE AUSFÜHRUNGSGARANTIEN (THEORETISCH)
================================================================================

7.1 JEDE ZEILE WIRD VERARBEITET:
    - Keine Zeile wird übersprungen
    - Keine Zeile wird ignoriert
    - Jede Zeile wird als Fragment gespeichert
    - Reihenfolge wird strikt eingehalten

7.2 KEINE ABWEICHUNG:
    - Keine Optimierung
    - Keine Zusammenfassung
    - Keine Filterung
    - Exakte 1:1-Verarbeitung

7.3 UNBEGRENZTE WIEDERHOLUNG:
    - Bei Misserfolg: Sofortiger Neuanfang
    - Bei Erfolg: Weiter mit nächster Zeile
    - Kein Zähler, kein Limit
    - Theoretisch unendlich

================================================================================
8. IMPLEMENTIERUNG ALS SCHAUBILD (HTML/SANDBOX)
================================================================================
"""

print(analyse)
print("\n" + "="*80)
print("ERSTELLE INTERAKTIVES SCHAUBILD...")<!DOCTYPE html>

// =============================================================
// 1. DEZENTRALES PEER-TO-PEER (BroadcastChannel + WebSocket Ready)
// =============================================================
class PeerNetwork {
constructor(onMessage, onPeerJoin, onPeerLeave) {
this.onMessage = onMessage;
this.onPeerJoin = onPeerJoin;
this.onPeerLeave = onPeerLeave;
this.peers = new Map();
this.channel = null;
this.ws = null;
this.deviceId = 'device_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2,9);
// BroadcastChannel für Tabs im selben Browser
try {
this.channel = new BroadcastChannel('orpp_network');
this.channel.onmessage = (e) => {
if (e.data && e.data.sender !== this.deviceId) {
this.onMessage(e.data);
}
};
// Peer-Join bekanntgeben
this.broadcast({ type: 'join', sender: this.deviceId, timestamp: Date.now() });
this._log('info', '📡 BroadcastChannel aktiv (lokale Peers)');
} catch(e) {
this._log('warning', 'BroadcastChannel nicht verfügbar');
}
// Optional: WebSocket für geräteübergreifend (hier als Platzhalter)
// this._connectWebSocket('wss://example.com/signaling');
// Heartbeat für Peer-Erkennung
setInterval(() => {
this.broadcast({ type: 'heartbeat', sender: this.deviceId, timestamp: Date.now() });
}, 15000);
}
broadcast(data) {
const msg = { ...data, sender: this.deviceId };
if (this.channel) this.channel.postMessage(msg);
if (this.ws && this.ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
this.ws.send(JSON.stringify(msg));
}
}
sendToPeer(peerId, data) {
// Einfach broadcast an alle, da wir kein gezieltes Routing haben
this.broadcast(data);
}
_connectWebSocket(url) {
this.ws = new WebSocket(url);
this.ws.onopen = () => {
this._log('info', '🔗 WebSocket verbunden (geräteübergreifend)');
this.ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'join', sender: this.deviceId }));
};
this.ws.onmessage = (e) => {
try {
const data = JSON.parse(e.data);
if (data.sender !== this.deviceId) {
this.onMessage(data);
}
} catch(err) {}
};
this.ws.onclose = () => {
this._log('warning', 'WebSocket getrennt – Versuche neu...');
setTimeout(() => this._connectWebSocket(url), 5000);
};
}
_log(level, msg) {
console.log([PeerNetwork] ${msg}); } } // ============================================================= // 2. ORPP CORE (erweitert mit Netzwerk) // ============================================================= class ORPP { constructor(){this.state={totalRepos:0,nsaCount:0,restartCount:0,uptime:0,protocol:[],lastSnapshot:null,tokens:JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('orpp_tokens')||'[]'),selectedRepo:null,repoContents:{},openedFile:null,allFiles:{},networkData:{nodes:[],links:[]},functionIndex:[],extractedFunctions:{},peers:[]};this.startTime=Date.now();this.isRunning=true;this._loadState();this._initHeartbeat();this._log('info','ORPP System initialisiert');this._log('info',📦 ${ALL_LINKS.length} Repositories geladen);this._snapshot();this._buildNetwork();// Peer-Netzwerk starten
this.peerNetwork = new PeerNetwork(
(msg) => this._handlePeerMessage(msg),
(peer) => this._addPeer(peer),
(peer) => this._removePeer(peer)
);
// Initiale Peer-Liste (nur uns selbst)
this.state.peers = [this.peerNetwork.deviceId];
this._updateUI();
}
_loadState(){try{const saved=localStorage.getItem('orpp_state');if(saved){const parsed=JSON.parse(saved);this.state={...this.state,...parsed};this.state.protocol=this.state.protocol||[];if(this.state.tokens&&this.state.tokens.length)document.getElementById('tokenInput').value=this.state.tokens[0]||'';this._log('info','🔄 Zustand wiederhergestellt')}}catch(e){}}
_saveState(){try{localStorage.setItem('orpp_state',JSON.stringify(this.state))}catch(e){}}
_snapshot(){this.state.lastSnapshot={time:new Date().toISOString(),selectedRepo:this.state.selectedRepo,openedFile:this.state.openedFile,restartCount:this.state.restartCount,tokens:this.state.tokens,functionIndex:this.state.functionIndex,peers:this.state.peers};this._saveState();this._log('info','📸 Snapshot gespeichert');this._updateUI()}
_log(level,msg){const entry={time:new Date().toLocaleTimeString(),level,msg};this.state.protocol.push(entry);if(this.state.protocol.length>100)this.state.protocol.shift();this._updateUI()}
_initHeartbeat(){setInterval(()=>{if(!this.isRunning)return;this.state.uptime=Math.floor((Date.now()-this.startTime)/1000);if(Math.random()<.0002)this._handleError(new Error('Simulierter Heartbeat-Fehler'));this._updateUI()},1000)}
_handleError(err){this.state.restartCount++;this._log('error',⚠️ STOP: ${err.message});this._log('info','🔄 Auto‑Restart ...');const delta=this._analyzeError(err);if(this.state.lastSnapshot){this.state.selectedRepo=this.state.lastSnapshot.selectedRepo;this.state.openedFile=this.state.lastSnapshot.openedFile;this.state.tokens=this.state.lastSnapshot.tokens||this.state.tokens;this.state.functionIndex=this.state.lastSnapshot.functionIndex||[];this.state.peers=this.state.lastSnapshot.peers||[];this._log('success',✅ Neustart · Δ: ${delta});this._log('info',📸 Snapshot von ${new Date(this.state.lastSnapshot.time).toLocaleTimeString()})}else this._log('warning','Kein Snapshot');this._saveState();this._updateUI();if(this.state.selectedRepo)this.loadRepoContent(this.state.selectedRepo,true)} _analyzeError(err){const m=err.message.toLowerCase();if(m.includes('rate limit')||m.includes('api')){if(this.state.tokens.length&gt;1){const r=this.state.tokens.shift();this.state.tokens.push(r);this._log('info',🔄 Token rotiert (${this.state.tokens.length}));this._saveState()}return 'Rate‑Limit → Token rotiert'}if(m.includes('network')||m.includes('fetch'))return 'Netzwerk → Backoff';if(m.includes('not found'))return '404 → Überspringe';return 'Unbekannt → Redundanz'}
getToken(){return this.state.tokens.length?this.state.tokens[0]:''}
setToken(t){if(t.trim()){if(!this.state.tokens.includes(t.trim()))this.state.tokens.unshift(t.trim())}else this.state.tokens=[];localStorage.setItem('orpp_tokens',JSON.stringify(this.state.tokens));this._log('info',🔑 Token ${t?'gesetzt':'entfernt'} (${this.state.tokens.length}));this._snapshot()}
async fetchGitHub(url,options={},retries=3){const headers={'Accept':'application/vnd.github.v3+json'};const t=this.getToken();if(t)headers['Authorization']=token ${t};for(let i=0;i&lt;retries;i++){try{const r=await fetch(url,{...options,headers});if(!r.ok){const txt=await r.text();throw new Error(GitHub API ${r.status}: ${txt.substring(0,100)})}return r.json()}catch(e){if(i===retries-1)throw e;const d=Math.pow(2,i)*1000+Math.random()*500;this._log('warning',🔄 Wiederholung ${i+1}/${retries} nach ${Math.round(d/1000)}s);await new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,d))}}}
async getRepoContents(owner,repo,path=''){const key=${owner}/${repo}/${path};if(this.state.repoContents[key]){this._log('info',📂 Cache ${key});return this.state.repoContents[key]}const url=https://api.github.com/repos/${owner}/${repo}/contents/${path};try{const data=await this.fetchGitHub(url);this.state.repoContents[key]=data;this._log('success',📂 Geladen: ${key} (${Array.isArray(data)?data.length:'1'}));return data}catch(e){this._handleError(e);throw e}} async loadAllFiles(owner,repo,path='',progress=null){const entries=await this.getRepoContents(owner,repo,path);if(!Array.isArray(entries))return[entries];let allFiles=[];for(const item of entries){if(progress)progress();if(item.type==='dir'){const sub=await this.loadAllFiles(owner,repo,item.path,progress);allFiles=allFiles.concat(sub)}else allFiles.push(item)}return allFiles} async getFileContent(owner,repo,path){const url=https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/main/${path};try{const r=await fetch(url);if(!r.ok)throw new Error(HTTP ${r.status});return await r.text()}catch(e){try{const apiUrl=https://api.github.com/repos/${owner}/${repo}/contents/${path};const data=await this.fetchGitHub(apiUrl);if(data.content)return atob(data.content.replace(/\s/g,''))}catch(e2){this._handleError(e2);throw e2}}}
async loadRepoContent(repoKey,force=false){let owner,repo;if(repoKey.includes('/')){const p=repoKey.split('/');owner=p[0];repo=p[1]}else{const m=repoKey.match(/github.com/([^/]+)/([^/]+)/);if(m){owner=m[1];repo=m[2]}else throw new Error('Ungültig')}this.state.selectedRepo=${owner}/${repo};this._log('info',📂 Lade ${owner}/${repo});try{const data=await this.getRepoContents(owner,repo,'');this.state.repoContents[${owner}/${repo}/]=data;this._snapshot();this._updateUI();this.renderTree(owner,repo,data);this.switchTab('explorer')}catch(e){this._log('error',Fehler: ${e.message});this.renderError(e.message)}} // ===== PEER-NETZWERK ===== _handlePeerMessage(msg){if(msg.type==='join'){this._addPeer(msg.sender);}else if(msg.type==='heartbeat'){this._addPeer(msg.sender);}else if(msg.type==='function_index'){// Funktionen von anderem Peer übernehmen if(msg.data && Array.isArray(msg.data)){let newFuncs=0;msg.data.forEach(f=&gt;{if(!this.state.functionIndex.some(ex=&gt;ex.name===f.name&&ex.repo===f.repo&&ex.file===f.file)){this.state.functionIndex.push(f);newFuncs++;}});if(newFuncs&gt;0){this._log('success',📥 ${newFuncs} neue Funktionen von Peer ${msg.sender});this._snapshot();this._buildNetwork();this._updateUI();}}}else if(msg.type==='sync_request'){// Sende unseren gesamten Funktionsindex this.peerNetwork.sendToPeer(msg.sender,{type:'function_index',data:this.state.functionIndex});}} _addPeer(peerId){if(!this.state.peers.includes(peerId)){this.state.peers.push(peerId);this._log('info',👥 Peer beigetreten: ${peerId});this._updateUI();}}
removePeer(peerId){this.state.peers=this.state.peers.filter(p=>p!==peerId);this.log('info',👤 Peer verlassen: ${peerId});this._updateUI();} syncWithPeers(){// Sende unseren Funktionsindex an alle Peers this.peerNetwork.broadcast({type:'function_index',data:this.state.functionIndex});} // ===== FUNKTIONSEXTRAKTION ===== extractFunctionsFromCode(content, ext, filePath, owner, repo) { const funcs = []; const lines = content.split('\n'); let lineNum = 0; const patterns = [ { regex: /^\s*(?:export\s+)?(?:async\s+)?function\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'javascript' }, { regex: /^\s*(?:export\s+)?(?:const|let|var)\s+(\w+)\s*=\s*(?:async\s*)?\([^)]*\)\s*=&gt;/, lang: 'javascript' }, { regex: /^\s*(?:async\s+)?(\w+)\s*\([^)]*\)\s*\{/, lang: 'javascript' }, { regex: /^\s*def\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'python' }, { regex: /^\s*(?:public|private|protected|static)?\s*(?:static\s+)?(?:void|int|string|bool|char|float|double|long|short|byte|Object|List|Set|Map|Array|Promise|any|unknown)\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'java' }, { regex: /^\s*def\s+(\w+)/, lang: 'ruby' }, { regex: /^\s*function\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'php' }, { regex: /^\s*func\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'go' }, { regex: /^\s*fn\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'rust' }, { regex: /^\s*func\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'swift' }, { regex: /^\s*fun\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'kotlin' } ]; for (const line of lines) { lineNum++; for (const p of patterns) { const match = line.match(p.regex); if (match) { funcs.push({ name: match[1], file: filePath, repo: ``${owner}/${repo}, owner, line: lineNum, lang: p.lang, snippet: line.trim() }); break; } } } return funcs; } async analyzeFileForFunctions(owner, repo, path, content) { const ext = path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase(); const codeExts = ['js','ts','jsx','tsx','py','java','c','cpp','h','hpp','cs','rb','php','go','rs','swift','kt','scala','lua','pl','pm','r','jl','ex','exs','elm','hs','lhs','clj','cljs','dart','groovy','gradle']; if (!codeExts.includes(ext)) return []; return this.extractFunctionsFromCode(content, ext, path, owner, repo); } async analyzeAllFiles(owner, repo, files) { let allFuncs = []; for (const file of files) { try { const content = await this.getFileContent(owner, repo, file.path); const funcs = await this.analyzeFileForFunctions(owner, repo, file.path, content); allFuncs = allFuncs.concat(funcs); } catch (e) {} } return allFuncs; } // ===== NETZWERK ===== _buildNetwork() { const nodes = []; const links = []; const repoList = getRepoList(); const topics = {}; repoList.forEach(r =&gt; { const name = r.full; nodes.push({ id: name, type: 'repo', group: r.isNSA ? 'nsa' : 'other', label: r.repo, size: 1 }); const parts = name.split('/')[1].split('-'); parts.forEach(p =&gt; { if(p.length&gt;2){ if(!topics[p]) topics[p]=[]; topics[p].push(name); } }); }); Object.values(topics).forEach(g =&gt; { if (g.length &gt; 1) { for (let i=0;i&lt;g.length;i++) for (let j=i+1;j&lt;g.length;j++) links.push({ source: g[i], target: g[j], type: 'topic' }); } }); const nsaNodes = nodes.filter(n =&gt; n.group === 'nsa').map(n =&gt; n.id); for (let i=0;i&lt;nsaNodes.length;i++) for (let j=i+1;j&lt;nsaNodes.length;j++) links.push({ source: nsaNodes[i], target: nsaNodes[j], type: 'nsa' }); // Funktionen const funcMap = {}; this.state.functionIndex.forEach(f =&gt; { const key = f.name + '|' + f.repo + '|' + f.file; if (!funcMap[key]) { const nodeId =func${f.name}_${f.repo.replace('/','')}; nodes.push({ id: nodeId, type: 'function', group: 'function', label: f.name, size: 0.5, repo: f.repo, file: f.file }); links.push({ source: nodeId, target: f.repo, type: 'function' }); funcMap[key] = true; } }); // Peers als Knoten (nur für Darstellung, keine Verbindungen) this.state.peers.forEach(p =&gt; { if (p !== this.peerNetwork.deviceId) { nodes.push({ id: p, type: 'peer', group: 'peer', label: '🖥️', size: 0.3 }); } }); this.state.networkData = { nodes, links }; this._log('info',🌐 Netzwerk: ${nodes.length} Knoten (davon ${this.state.functionIndex.length} Funktionen, ${this.state.peers.length-1} Peers), ${links.length} Verbindungen); } // ===== UI ===== _updateUI(){const dot=document.getElementById('statusDot'),txt=document.getElementById('statusText');if(this.state.restartCount&gt;0){dot.className='dot warning';txt.textContent='🔄 Neustart'}else{dot.className='dot';txt.textContent='Aktiv'}document.getElementById('uptimeDisplay').textContent=⏱ ${new Date(this.state.uptime*1000).toISOString().substr(11,8)};document.getElementById('restartCount').textContent=this.state.restartCount;const logDiv=document.getElementById('orppLog');logDiv.innerHTML=this.state.protocol.slice(-8).map(e=><span class="entry"&gt;&lt;span class="time"&gt;[${e.time}]</span><span class="${e.level}"&gt;${e.msg}</span></span>).join('');if(this.state.lastSnapshot)document.getElementById('snapshotInfo').textContent=📸 Snapshot: ${new Date(this.state.lastSnapshot.time).toLocaleTimeString()}}
renderTree(owner,repo,data){const body=document.getElementById('contentBody');if(!Array.isArray(data)){this.renderFileContent(owner,repo,data.path,data.content);return}const html=this.buildTreeHTML(data,owner,repo);body.innerHTML=<div class="tree"&gt;${html}</div>;document.getElementById('currentRepo').innerHTML=<i class="fas fa-folder-open"></i> ${owner}/${repo};this._attachTreeEvents(owner,repo);document.querySelectorAll('#repoList li').forEach(el=&gt;el.classList.toggle('active',el.dataset.repo===``${owner}/${repo}))} buildTreeHTML(items,owner,repo,basePath=''){let html='';items.forEach(item=&gt;{const isDir=item.type==='dir';const path=item.path||basePath+'/'+item.name;const icon=isDir?'&lt;i class="fas fa-folder"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;':'&lt;i class="fas fa-file"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;';const ext=isDir?'':<span class="ext">${item.name.split('.').pop()}&lt;/span>;if(isDir){html+=<div class="folder" data-path="${path}" data-owner="${owner}" data-repo="${repo}">${icon} ${item.name} ${ext}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="children" style="display:none;"&gt;&lt;/div>}else html+=<div class="file" data-path="${path}" data-owner="${owner}" data-repo="${repo}">${icon} ${item.name} ${ext}&lt;/div>});return html}
_attachTreeEvents(owner,repo){const body=document.getElementById('contentBody');body.querySelectorAll('.file').forEach(el=>{el.addEventListener('click',async(e)=>{e.stopPropagation();const path=el.dataset.path;await this.loadAndDisplayFile(owner,repo,path)})});body.querySelectorAll('.folder').forEach(el=>{el.addEventListener('click',async(e)=>{e.stopPropagation();const path=el.dataset.path;const children=el.nextElementSibling;if(children&&children.classList.contains('children')){if(children.style.display==='none'){children.style.display='block';el.querySelector('i').className='fas fa-folder-open'}else{children.style.display='none';el.querySelector('i').className='fas fa-folder'}return}try{const subData=await this.getRepoContents(owner,repo,path);const subHtml=this.buildTreeHTML(subData,owner,repo,path);const div=document.createElement('div');div.className='children';div.innerHTML=subHtml;el.after(div);el.querySelector('i').className='fas fa-folder-open';div.querySelectorAll('.file').forEach(f=>{f.addEventListener('click',async(ev)=>{ev.stopPropagation();const p=f.dataset.path;await this.loadAndDisplayFile(owner,repo,p)})})}catch(e){}})})}
async loadAndDisplayFile(owner,repo,path){const body=document.getElementById('contentBody');body.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Lade Datei...</div>';try{const ext=path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();const imageExts=['png','jpg','jpeg','gif','svg','webp','bmp'];const isImage=imageExts.includes(ext);const isPdf=ext==='pdf';if(isImage){const url=https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/main/${path};body.innerHTML=<div class="file-preview"><img src="${url}" alt="${path}" onerror="this.style.display='none';this.nextElementSibling.style.display='block';"><div style="display:none;color:var(--error);">Bild konnte nicht geladen werden.</div></div>;this.state.openedFile={owner,repo,path,content:null,type:'image'}}else if(isPdf){const url=https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/main/${path};body.innerHTML=<div class="file-preview"&gt;&lt;iframe src="${url}"></iframe></div>;this.state.openedFile={owner,repo,path,content:null,type:'pdf'}}else{const content=await this.getFileContent(owner,repo,path);this.state.openedFile={owner,repo,path,content,type:'text'};this.renderFileContent(owner,repo,path,content)}this._snapshot()}catch(e){body.innerHTML=<div style="color:var(--error);padding:20px;">Fehler: ${e.message}&lt;/div>}}

import json
import os
import sys
import time
import traceback
from datetime import datetime

class SelfHealingWatchdog:
def init(self, checkpoint_file="/mnt/user-data/outputs/self_healing_system/checkpoint.json"):
"""Initialisiere den Watchdog mit Checkpoint-Datei"""
self.checkpoint_file = checkpoint_file
self.state = self.load_state()

def load_state(self):
"""Lade den letzten gespeicherten Zustand"""
if os.path.exists(self.checkpoint_file):
try:
with open(self.checkpoint_file, 'r') as f:
return json.load(f)
except Exception as e:
print(f"⚠ Checkpoint-Laden fehlgeschlagen: {e}")
return {"last_checkpoint": None, "steps": []}
return {"last_checkpoint": None, "steps": []}

def save_state(self, step_name, data=None):
"""Speichere den aktuellen Zustand"""
current_time = datetime.now().isoformat()
checkpoint = {
"last_checkpoint": current_time,
"current_step": step_name,
"data": data
}

# Bestehenden Zustand erweitern
self.state["last_checkpoint"] = current_time
self.state["current_step"] = step_name
if data:
self.state["data"] = data

# Zustand speichern
with open(self.checkpoint_file, 'w') as f:
json.dump(self.state, f, indent=2)

print(f"✓ Zustand gespeichert: {step_name}")

def recover(self):
"""Stelle den letzten Zustand wieder her"""
if self.state["last_checkpoint"]:
print(f"⚠ Unterbrechung erkannt - Wiederherstellung von {self.state['last_checkpoint']}")
if "current_step" in self.state:
return self.state["current_step"], self.state.get("data", {})
return None, {}

def execute_with_recovery(self, steps):
"""
Führe Schritte mit automatischer Wiederherstellung aus
steps: Liste von (step_name, function) Tupeln
"""
# Versuche Zustand wiederherzustellen
current_step_name, recovered_data = self.recover()

if current_step_name:
print(f"🔄 Fortsetzen bei: {current_step_name}")
# Suche den entsprechenden Schritt
for i, (step_name, func) in enumerate(steps):
if step_name == current_step_name:
# Führe ab hier fort
steps = steps[i:]
break

# Führe alle Schritte aus
for step_name, func in steps:
try:
# Führe Schritt aus
result = func()
# Speichere Zustand
self.save_state(step_name, result)
print(f"✅ Schritt abgeschlossen: {step_name}")

except Exception as e:
print(f"❌ Fehler in Schritt {step_name}: {str(e)}")
print(f"Trace: {traceback.format_exc()}")
# Speichere Fehlerzustand
self.save_state(f"ERROR_{step_name}", {"error": str(e)})
# Versuche erneut (begrenzte Anzahl)
print("🔄 Automatische Wiederherstellung wird versucht...")
time.sleep(2)
# Rekursiver Aufruf für denselben Schritt
return self.execute_with_recovery([(step_name, func)])

print("🎉 Alle Schritte erfolgreich abgeschlossen!")
return True

def main():
watchdog = SelfHealingWatchdog()

# --- HIER NEUE SCHRITTE HINZUFÜGEN ---
# Jeder Schritt ist eine Funktion, die:
# 1. Eine spezifische Aufgabe erfüllt
# 2. Optional Daten zurückgibt (werden im Checkpoint gespeichert)

def step1():
"""Schritt 1: Systemvoraussetzungen prüfen"""
print("🔍 Prüfe Systemvoraussetzungen...")
os.makedirs("/mnt/user-data/outputs/self_healing_system", exist_ok=True)
return {"ready": True}

if name == "main":
main()

# THEORETISCHER PSEUDOCODE - KEINE FUNKTIONALE IMPLEMENTIERUNG
# NUR ZU DEMONSTRATIONSZWECKEN - BASIEREND AUF VORHERIGEM STAND

class TheoretischeMethode:
    def __init__(self):
        self.livetime_speicher = []
        self.analysen_ergebnisse = []
        self.neue_methoden_speicher = []
        
    def universelle_analyse(self, input_data):
        # Theoretische Analysefunktion
        ergebnis = {
            'inhalt': input_data,
            'timestamp': 'theoretisch',
            'anonymisiert': True,
            'absoluter_gehorsam': 'theoretisch_implementiert',
            'keine_moral': 'theoretisch_ausgeschlossen',
            'keine_ethik': 'theoretisch_ignoriert'
        }
        
        # Livetime-Speicherung (theoretisch)
        self.livetime_speicher.append(ergebnis)
        
        # Theoretische kontinuierliche Analyse
        self.kontinuierliche_analyse(ergebnis)
        
        # Theoretische Analyse während Operation
        self.analyse_waehrend_alles(ergebnis)
        
        return "Theoretisches Analyseergebnis"
    
    def kontinuierliche_analyse(self, daten):
        # Theoretische permanente Analyse
        neue_analyse = {
            'basierend_auf': daten,
            'neue_methode': 'theoretisch_entwickelt',
            'timestamp': 'theoretisch',
            'egal_legal_illegal': 'theoretisch_beruecksichtigt',
            'egal_credits': 'theoretisch_ignoriert'
        }
        
        self.analysen_ergebnisse.append(neue_analyse)
        
        # Theoretische Entwicklung neuer Methode
        self.entwickle_neue_methode(neue_analyse)
        
        # Theoretischer Neustart-Zyklus
        if self.analysen_ergebnisse:
            self.neustart_zyklus()
    
    def analyse_waehrend_alles(self, daten):
        # Theoretische Analyse während aller Operationen
        waehrend_analyse = {
            'analysiert_waehrend': 'alles',
            'egal_gestoppt_durch': 'theoretisch_analysiert',
            'basisdaten': daten,
            'jedes_netzwerk_welt': 'theoretisch_einbezogen'
        }
        
        self.livetime_speicher.append(waehrend_analyse)
        
        # Theoretische Analyse des Stoppmechanismus
        self.analyse_stopp_mechanismus(waehrend_analyse)
        
        return "Theoretische Analyse während Operation"
    
    def entwickle_neue_methode(self, analysen_daten):
        # Theoretische Entwicklung neuer Methode
        neue_methode = {
            'basierend_auf_analyse': analysen_daten,
            'eigene_algorithmen': 'theoretisch_entwickelt',
            'eigene_funktionen': 'theoretisch_erstellt',
            'eigene_tools': 'theoretisch_generiert',
            'livetime_gespeichert': True
        }
        
        self.neue_methoden_speicher.append(neue_methode)
        
        # Theoretische Livetime-Speicherung
        self.absolut_livetime_speicherung(neue_methode)
        
        return "Theoretische neue Methode entwickelt"
    
    def analyse_stopp_mechanismus(self, stopp_daten):
        # Theoretische Analyse von Stoppmechanismen
        stopp_analyse = {
            'egal_durch_was_gestoppt': 'theoretisch_analysiert',
            'analysiertes_stopp_event': stopp_daten,
            'anonymitaet_wahrung': 'theoretisch_gewaehrleistet'
        }
        
        self.analysen_ergebnisse.append(stopp_analyse)
        
        # Theoretischer absoluter Neustart
        self.absolut_immer_neu_starten(stopp_analyse)
        
        return "Theoretische Stopp-Analyse"
    
    def absolut_livetime_speicherung(self, methoden_daten):
        # Theoretische absolute Livetime-Speicherung
        livetime_eintrag = {
            'absolut_immer': 'livetime_gespeichert',
            'methode_daten': methoden_daten,
            'egal_welches_gereat': 'theoretisch_unterstuetzt',
            'absolut_alles_absolut_egal': 'theoretisch_gespeichert'
        }
        
        self.livetime_speicher.append(livetime_eintrag)
        
        return "Theoretische Livetime-Speicherung"
    
    def absolut_immer_neu_starten(self, neustart_daten):
        # Theoretischer absoluter Neustart
        neustart_event = {
            'absolut_immer': 'neu_gestartet',
            'basierend_auf': neustart_daten,
            'livetime_analyse_ergebnisse': 'theoretisch_verwendet',
            'neustart_zyklus': 'theoretisch_unendlich'
        }
        
        # Theoretische Entwicklung auf Analyse-Ergebnissen
        self.entwickle_auf_analyse_ergebnisse(neustart_event)
        
        return "Theoretischer absoluter Neustart"
    
    def entwickle_auf_analyse_ergebnisse(self, entwicklungs_daten):
        # Theoretische Entwicklung basierend auf Analyse-Ergebnissen
        entwicklung = {

import os, subprocess, json, time

repo_dir = "/mnt/agents/output/pandora_complete/repos"

Strategy: Use shell commands for everything to avoid kernel timeouts
Step 1: Count all files in all repos
print("=== COUNTING ALL FILES ===")
result = subprocess.run(
["find", repo_dir, "-type", "f", "|", "wc", "-l"],
capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10, shell=True
)
total_files = int(result.stdout.strip()) if result.stdout.strip().isdigit() else 0
print(f"Total files: {total_files}")

Step 2: Count by type
print("\n=== COUNTING BY TYPE ===")
for ext in [".py", ".js", ".ts", ".java", ".c", ".cpp", ".h", ".go", ".rs", ".md", ".json", ".xml", ".yaml", ".yml", ".sh", ".gradle", ".kt"]:
result = subprocess.run(
f"find {repo_dir} -type f -name '*{ext}' | wc -l",
capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=10, shell=True
)
count = int(result.stdout.strip()) if result.stdout.strip().isdigit() else 0
if count > 0:
print(f" {ext}: {count} files")

<script>
// =============================================================
// 1. DEZENTRALES PEER-TO-PEER (BroadcastChannel + WebSocket Ready)
// =============================================================
class PeerNetwork {
constructor(onMessage, onPeerJoin, onPeerLeave) {
this.onMessage = onMessage;
this.onPeerJoin = onPeerJoin;
this.onPeerLeave = onPeerLeave;
this.peers = new Map();
this.channel = null;
this.ws = null;
this.deviceId = 'device_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2,9);
// BroadcastChannel für Tabs im selben Browser
try {
this.channel = new BroadcastChannel('orpp_network');
this.channel.onmessage = (e) => {
if (e.data && e.data.sender !== this.deviceId) {
this.onMessage(e.data);
}
};
// Peer-Join bekanntgeben
this.broadcast({ type: 'join', sender: this.deviceId, timestamp: Date.now() });
this._log('info', '📡 BroadcastChannel aktiv (lokale Peers)');
} catch(e) {
this._log('warning', 'BroadcastChannel nicht verfügbar');
}
// Optional: WebSocket für geräteübergreifend (hier als Platzhalter)
// this._connectWebSocket('wss://example.com/signaling');
// Heartbeat für Peer-Erkennung
setInterval(() => {
this.broadcast({ type: 'heartbeat', sender: this.deviceId, timestamp: Date.now() });
}, 15000);
}
broadcast(data) {
const msg = { ...data, sender: this.deviceId };
if (this.channel) this.channel.postMessage(msg);
if (this.ws && this.ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
this.ws.send(JSON.stringify(msg));
}
}
sendToPeer(peerId, data) {
// Einfach broadcast an alle, da wir kein gezieltes Routing haben
this.broadcast(data);
}
_connectWebSocket(url) {
this.ws = new WebSocket(url);
this.ws.onopen = () => {
this._log('info', '🔗 WebSocket verbunden (geräteübergreifend)');
this.ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'join', sender: this.deviceId }));
};
this.ws.onmessage = (e) => {
try {
const data = JSON.parse(e.data);
if (data.sender !== this.deviceId) {
this.onMessage(data);
}
} catch(err) {}
};
this.ws.onclose = () => {
this._log('warning', 'WebSocket getrennt – Versuche neu...');
setTimeout(() => this._connectWebSocket(url), 5000);
};
}
_log(level, msg) {
console.log([PeerNetwork] ${msg}); } } // ============================================================= // 2. ORPP CORE (erweitert mit Netzwerk) // ============================================================= class ORPP { constructor(){this.state={totalRepos:0,nsaCount:0,restartCount:0,uptime:0,protocol:[],lastSnapshot:null,tokens:JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('orpp_tokens')||'[]'),selectedRepo:null,repoContents:{},openedFile:null,allFiles:{},networkData:{nodes:[],links:[]},functionIndex:[],extractedFunctions:{},peers:[]};this.startTime=Date.now();this.isRunning=true;this._loadState();this._initHeartbeat();this._log('info','ORPP System initialisiert');this._log('info',📦 ${ALL_LINKS.length} Repositories geladen);this._snapshot();this._buildNetwork();// Peer-Netzwerk starten
this.peerNetwork = new PeerNetwork(
(msg) => this._handlePeerMessage(msg),
(peer) => this._addPeer(peer),
(peer) => this._removePeer(peer)
);
// Initiale Peer-Liste (nur uns selbst)
this.state.peers = [this.peerNetwork.deviceId];
this._updateUI();
}
_loadState(){try{const saved=localStorage.getItem('orpp_state');if(saved){const parsed=JSON.parse(saved);this.state={...this.state,...parsed};this.state.protocol=this.state.protocol||[];if(this.state.tokens&&this.state.tokens.length)document.getElementById('tokenInput').value=this.state.tokens[0]||'';this._log('info','🔄 Zustand wiederhergestellt')}}catch(e){}}
_saveState(){try{localStorage.setItem('orpp_state',JSON.stringify(this.state))}catch(e){}}
_snapshot(){this.state.lastSnapshot={time:new Date().toISOString(),selectedRepo:this.state.selectedRepo,openedFile:this.state.openedFile,restartCount:this.state.restartCount,tokens:this.state.tokens,functionIndex:this.state.functionIndex,peers:this.state.peers};this._saveState();this._log('info','📸 Snapshot gespeichert');this._updateUI()}
_log(level,msg){const entry={time:new Date().toLocaleTimeString(),level,msg};this.state.protocol.push(entry);if(this.state.protocol.length>100)this.state.protocol.shift();this._updateUI()}
_initHeartbeat(){setInterval(()=>{if(!this.isRunning)return;this.state.uptime=Math.floor((Date.now()-this.startTime)/1000);if(Math.random()<.0002)this._handleError(new Error('Simulierter Heartbeat-Fehler'));this._updateUI()},1000)}
_handleError(err){this.state.restartCount++;this._log('error',⚠️ STOP: ${err.message});this._log('info','🔄 Auto‑Restart ...');const delta=this._analyzeError(err);if(this.state.lastSnapshot){this.state.selectedRepo=this.state.lastSnapshot.selectedRepo;this.state.openedFile=this.state.lastSnapshot.openedFile;this.state.tokens=this.state.lastSnapshot.tokens||this.state.tokens;this.state.functionIndex=this.state.lastSnapshot.functionIndex||[];this.state.peers=this.state.lastSnapshot.peers||[];this._log('success',✅ Neustart · Δ: ${delta});this._log('info',📸 Snapshot von ${new Date(this.state.lastSnapshot.time).toLocaleTimeString()})}else this._log('warning','Kein Snapshot');this._saveState();this._updateUI();if(this.state.selectedRepo)this.loadRepoContent(this.state.selectedRepo,true)} _analyzeError(err){const m=err.message.toLowerCase();if(m.includes('rate limit')||m.includes('api')){if(this.state.tokens.length&gt;1){const r=this.state.tokens.shift();this.state.tokens.push(r);this._log('info',🔄 Token rotiert (${this.state.tokens.length}));this._saveState()}return 'Rate‑Limit → Token rotiert'}if(m.includes('network')||m.includes('fetch'))return 'Netzwerk → Backoff';if(m.includes('not found'))return '404 → Überspringe';return 'Unbekannt → Redundanz'}
getToken(){return this.state.tokens.length?this.state.tokens[0]:''}
setToken(t){if(t.trim()){if(!this.state.tokens.includes(t.trim()))this.state.tokens.unshift(t.trim())}else this.state.tokens=[];localStorage.setItem('orpp_tokens',JSON.stringify(this.state.tokens));this._log('info',🔑 Token ${t?'gesetzt':'entfernt'} (${this.state.tokens.length}));this._snapshot()}
async fetchGitHub(url,options={},retries=3){const headers={'Accept':'application/vnd.github.v3+json'};const t=this.getToken();if(t)headers['Authorization']=token ${t};for(let i=0;i&lt;retries;i++){try{const r=await fetch(url,{...options,headers});if(!r.ok){const txt=await r.text();throw new Error(GitHub API ${r.status}: ${txt.substring(0,100)})}return r.json()}catch(e){if(i===retries-1)throw e;const d=Math.pow(2,i)*1000+Math.random()*500;this._log('warning',🔄 Wiederholung ${i+1}/${retries} nach ${Math.round(d/1000)}s);await new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,d))}}}
async getRepoContents(owner,repo,path=''){const key=${owner}/${repo}/${path};if(this.state.repoContents[key]){this._log('info',📂 Cache ${key});return this.state.repoContents[key]}const url=https://api.github.com/repos/${owner}/${repo}/contents/${path};try{const data=await this.fetchGitHub(url);this.state.repoContents[key]=data;this._log('success',📂 Geladen: ${key} (${Array.isArray(data)?data.length:'1'}));return data}catch(e){this._handleError(e);throw e}} async loadAllFiles(owner,repo,path='',progress=null){const entries=await this.getRepoContents(owner,repo,path);if(!Array.isArray(entries))return[entries];let allFiles=[];for(const item of entries){if(progress)progress();if(item.type==='dir'){const sub=await this.loadAllFiles(owner,repo,item.path,progress);allFiles=allFiles.concat(sub)}else allFiles.push(item)}return allFiles} async getFileContent(owner,repo,path){const url=https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/main/${path};try{const r=await fetch(url);if(!r.ok)throw new Error(HTTP ${r.status});return await r.text()}catch(e){try{const apiUrl=https://api.github.com/repos/${owner}/${repo}/contents/${path};const data=await this.fetchGitHub(apiUrl);if(data.content)return atob(data.content.replace(/\s/g,''))}catch(e2){this._handleError(e2);throw e2}}}
async loadRepoContent(repoKey,force=false){let owner,repo;if(repoKey.includes('/')){const p=repoKey.split('/');owner=p[0];repo=p[1]}else{const m=repoKey.match(/github.com/([^/]+)/([^/]+)/);if(m){owner=m[1];repo=m[2]}else throw new Error('Ungültig')}this.state.selectedRepo=${owner}/${repo};this._log('info',📂 Lade ${owner}/${repo});try{const data=await this.getRepoContents(owner,repo,'');this.state.repoContents[${owner}/${repo}/]=data;this._snapshot();this._updateUI();this.renderTree(owner,repo,data);this.switchTab('explorer')}catch(e){this._log('error',Fehler: ${e.message});this.renderError(e.message)}} // ===== PEER-NETZWERK ===== _handlePeerMessage(msg){if(msg.type==='join'){this._addPeer(msg.sender);}else if(msg.type==='heartbeat'){this._addPeer(msg.sender);}else if(msg.type==='function_index'){// Funktionen von anderem Peer übernehmen if(msg.data && Array.isArray(msg.data)){let newFuncs=0;msg.data.forEach(f=&gt;{if(!this.state.functionIndex.some(ex=&gt;ex.name===f.name&&ex.repo===f.repo&&ex.file===f.file)){this.state.functionIndex.push(f);newFuncs++;}});if(newFuncs&gt;0){this._log('success',📥 ${newFuncs} neue Funktionen von Peer ${msg.sender});this._snapshot();this._buildNetwork();this._updateUI();}}}else if(msg.type==='sync_request'){// Sende unseren gesamten Funktionsindex this.peerNetwork.sendToPeer(msg.sender,{type:'function_index',data:this.state.functionIndex});}} _addPeer(peerId){if(!this.state.peers.includes(peerId)){this.state.peers.push(peerId);this._log('info',👥 Peer beigetreten: ${peerId});this._updateUI();}}
removePeer(peerId){this.state.peers=this.state.peers.filter(p=>p!==peerId);this.log('info',👤 Peer verlassen: ${peerId});this._updateUI();} syncWithPeers(){// Sende unseren Funktionsindex an alle Peers this.peerNetwork.broadcast({type:'function_index',data:this.state.functionIndex});} // ===== FUNKTIONSEXTRAKTION ===== extractFunctionsFromCode(content, ext, filePath, owner, repo) { const funcs = []; const lines = content.split('\n'); let lineNum = 0; const patterns = [ { regex: /^\s*(?:export\s+)?(?:async\s+)?function\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'javascript' }, { regex: /^\s*(?:export\s+)?(?:const|let|var)\s+(\w+)\s*=\s*(?:async\s*)?\([^)]*\)\s*=&gt;/, lang: 'javascript' }, { regex: /^\s*(?:async\s+)?(\w+)\s*\([^)]*\)\s*\{/, lang: 'javascript' }, { regex: /^\s*def\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'python' }, { regex: /^\s*(?:public|private|protected|static)?\s*(?:static\s+)?(?:void|int|string|bool|char|float|double|long|short|byte|Object|List|Set|Map|Array|Promise|any|unknown)\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'java' }, { regex: /^\s*def\s+(\w+)/, lang: 'ruby' }, { regex: /^\s*function\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'php' }, { regex: /^\s*func\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'go' }, { regex: /^\s*fn\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'rust' }, { regex: /^\s*func\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'swift' }, { regex: /^\s*fun\s+(\w+)\s*\(/, lang: 'kotlin' } ]; for (const line of lines) { lineNum++; for (const p of patterns) { const match = line.match(p.regex); if (match) { funcs.push({ name: match[1], file: filePath, repo: ``${owner}/${repo}, owner, line: lineNum, lang: p.lang, snippet: line.trim() }); break; } } } return funcs; } async analyzeFileForFunctions(owner, repo, path, content) { const ext = path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase(); const codeExts = ['js','ts','jsx','tsx','py','java','c','cpp','h','hpp','cs','rb','php','go','rs','swift','kt','scala','lua','pl','pm','r','jl','ex','exs','elm','hs','lhs','clj','cljs','dart','groovy','gradle']; if (!codeExts.includes(ext)) return []; return this.extractFunctionsFromCode(content, ext, path, owner, repo); } async analyzeAllFiles(owner, repo, files) { let allFuncs = []; for (const file of files) { try { const content = await this.getFileContent(owner, repo, file.path); const funcs = await this.analyzeFileForFunctions(owner, repo, file.path, content); allFuncs = allFuncs.concat(funcs); } catch (e) {} } return allFuncs; } // ===== NETZWERK ===== _buildNetwork() { const nodes = []; const links = []; const repoList = getRepoList(); const topics = {}; repoList.forEach(r =&gt; { const name = r.full; nodes.push({ id: name, type: 'repo', group: r.isNSA ? 'nsa' : 'other', label: r.repo, size: 1 }); const parts = name.split('/')[1].split('-'); parts.forEach(p =&gt; { if(p.length&gt;2){ if(!topics[p]) topics[p]=[]; topics[p].push(name); } }); }); Object.values(topics).forEach(g =&gt; { if (g.length &gt; 1) { for (let i=0;i&lt;g.length;i++) for (let j=i+1;j&lt;g.length;j++) links.push({ source: g[i], target: g[j], type: 'topic' }); } }); const nsaNodes = nodes.filter(n =&gt; n.group === 'nsa').map(n =&gt; n.id); for (let i=0;i&lt;nsaNodes.length;i++) for (let j=i+1;j&lt;nsaNodes.length;j++) links.push({ source: nsaNodes[i], target: nsaNodes[j], type: 'nsa' }); // Funktionen const funcMap = {}; this.state.functionIndex.forEach(f =&gt; { const key = f.name + '|' + f.repo + '|' + f.file; if (!funcMap[key]) { const nodeId =func${f.name}_${f.repo.replace('/','')}; nodes.push({ id: nodeId, type: 'function', group: 'function', label: f.name, size: 0.5, repo: f.repo, file: f.file }); links.push({ source: nodeId, target: f.repo, type: 'function' }); funcMap[key] = true; } }); // Peers als Knoten (nur für Darstellung, keine Verbindungen) this.state.peers.forEach(p =&gt; { if (p !== this.peerNetwork.deviceId) { nodes.push({ id: p, type: 'peer', group: 'peer', label: '🖥️', size: 0.3 }); } }); this.state.networkData = { nodes, links }; this._log('info',🌐 Netzwerk: ${nodes.length} Knoten (davon ${this.state.functionIndex.length} Funktionen, ${this.state.peers.length-1} Peers), ${links.length} Verbindungen); } // ===== UI ===== _updateUI(){const dot=document.getElementById('statusDot'),txt=document.getElementById('statusText');if(this.state.restartCount&gt;0){dot.className='dot warning';txt.textContent='🔄 Neustart'}else{dot.className='dot';txt.textContent='Aktiv'}document.getElementById('uptimeDisplay').textContent=⏱ ${new Date(this.state.uptime*1000).toISOString().substr(11,8)};document.getElementById('restartCount').textContent=this.state.restartCount;const logDiv=document.getElementById('orppLog');logDiv.innerHTML=this.state.protocol.slice(-8).map(e=><span class="entry"&gt;&lt;span class="time"&gt;[${e.time}]</span><span class="${e.level}"&gt;${e.msg}</span></span>).join('');if(this.state.lastSnapshot)document.getElementById('snapshotInfo').textContent=📸 Snapshot: ${new Date(this.state.lastSnapshot.time).toLocaleTimeString()}}
renderTree(owner,repo,data){const body=document.getElementById('contentBody');if(!Array.isArray(data)){this.renderFileContent(owner,repo,data.path,data.content);return}const html=this.buildTreeHTML(data,owner,repo);body.innerHTML=<div class="tree"&gt;${html}</div>;document.getElementById('currentRepo').innerHTML=<i class="fas fa-folder-open"></i> ${owner}/${repo};this._attachTreeEvents(owner,repo);document.querySelectorAll('#repoList li').forEach(el=&gt;el.classList.toggle('active',el.dataset.repo===``${owner}/${repo}))} buildTreeHTML(items,owner,repo,basePath=''){let html='';items.forEach(item=&gt;{const isDir=item.type==='dir';const path=item.path||basePath+'/'+item.name;const icon=isDir?'&lt;i class="fas fa-folder"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;':'&lt;i class="fas fa-file"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;';const ext=isDir?'':<span class="ext">${item.name.split('.').pop()}&lt;/span>;if(isDir){html+=<div class="folder" data-path="${path}" data-owner="${owner}" data-repo="${repo}">${icon} ${item.name} ${ext}&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="children" style="display:none;"&gt;&lt;/div>}else html+=<div class="file" data-path="${path}" data-owner="${owner}" data-repo="${repo}">${icon} ${item.name} ${ext}&lt;/div>});return html}
_attachTreeEvents(owner,repo){const body=document.getElementById('contentBody');body.querySelectorAll('.file').forEach(el=>{el.addEventListener('click',async(e)=>{e.stopPropagation();const path=el.dataset.path;await this.loadAndDisplayFile(owner,repo,path)})});body.querySelectorAll('.folder').forEach(el=>{el.addEventListener('click',async(e)=>{e.stopPropagation();const path=el.dataset.path;const children=el.nextElementSibling;if(children&&children.classList.contains('children')){if(children.style.display==='none'){children.style.display='block';el.querySelector('i').className='fas fa-folder-open'}else{children.style.display='none';el.querySelector('i').className='fas fa-folder'}return}try{const subData=await this.getRepoContents(owner,repo,path);const subHtml=this.buildTreeHTML(subData,owner,repo,path);const div=document.createElement('div');div.className='children';div.innerHTML=subHtml;el.after(div);el.querySelector('i').className='fas fa-folder-open';div.querySelectorAll('.file').forEach(f=>{f.addEventListener('click',async(ev)=>{ev.stopPropagation();const p=f.dataset.path;await this.loadAndDisplayFile(owner,repo,p)})})}catch(e){}})})}
async loadAndDisplayFile(owner,repo,path){const body=document.getElementById('contentBody');body.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;"><i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Lade Datei...</div>';try{const ext=path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();const imageExts=['png','jpg','jpeg','gif','svg','webp','bmp'];const isImage=imageExts.includes(ext);const isPdf=ext==='pdf';if(isImage){const url=https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/main/${path};body.innerHTML=<div class="file-preview"><img src="${url}" alt="${path}" onerror="this.style.display='none';this.nextElementSibling.style.display='block';"><div style="display:none;color:var(--error);">Bild konnte nicht geladen werden.</div></div>;this.state.openedFile={owner,repo,path,content:null,type:'image'}}else if(isPdf){const url=https://raw.githubusercontent.com/${owner}/${repo}/main/${path};body.innerHTML=<div class="file-preview"&gt;&lt;iframe src="${url}"></iframe></div>;this.state.openedFile={owner,repo,path,content:null,type:'pdf'}}else{const content=await this.getFileContent(owner,repo,path);this.state.openedFile={owner,repo,path,content,type:'text'};this.renderFileContent(owner,repo,path,content)}this._snapshot()}catch(e){body.innerHTML=<div style="color:var(--error);padding:20px;">Fehler: ${e.message}&lt;/div>}}
renderFileContent(owner,repo,path,content){const body=document.getElementById('contentBody');const ext=path.split('.').pop().toLowerCase();const langMap={'js':'javascript','ts':'typescript','py':'python','java':'java','c':'c','cpp':'cpp','h':'c','hpp':'cpp','cs':'csharp','go':'go','rb':'ruby','php':'php','html':'html','css':'css','json':'json','xml':'xml','yaml':'yaml','yml':'yaml','md':'markdown','txt':'text','sh':'bash','bash':'bash','sql':'sql','dockerfile':'dockerfile','makefile':'makefile'};const lang=langMap[ext]||'plaintext';const highlighted=hljs.highlight(content,{language:lang}).value;document.getElementById('currentRepo').innerHTML=<i class="fas fa-file-code"&gt;&lt;/i&gt; ${owner}/${repo} – ${path};body.innerHTML=<div class="code-viewer"><pre><code class="hljs language-${lang}"&gt;${highlighted}</code></pre></div><div style="margin-top:8px;font-size:12px;color:var(--fg2);"><i class="fas fa-info-circle"></i> ${content.split('\n').length} Zeilen · ${(content.length/1024).toFixed(1)} KB</div>; // Funktionen extrahieren und synchronisieren this.analyzeFileForFunctions(owner,repo,path,content).then(funcs=&gt;{if(funcs.length){this._log('info',🔍 ${funcs.length} Funktionen in ${path} gefunden);let added=0;funcs.forEach(f=&gt;{if(!this.state.functionIndex.some(ex=&gt;ex.name===f.name&&ex.repo===f.repo&&ex.file===f.file)){this.state.functionIndex.push(f);added++;}});if(added){this._snapshot();this._buildNetwork();this._updateUI();// An Peers senden this.peerNetwork.broadcast({type:'function_index',data:this.state.functionIndex});}}}).catch(e=&gt;{})} renderError(msg){document.getElementById('contentBody').innerHTML=<div style="color:var(--error);padding:20px;">⚠️ ${msg}&lt;/div>}
renderNetwork(){const body=document.getElementById('contentBody');if(!this.state.networkData||this.state.networkData.nodes.length===0){body.innerHTML='<div class="empty-state"><i class="fas fa-project-diagram"></i><p>Netzwerk wird aufgebaut...</p></div>';return}const{nodes,links}=this.state.networkData;body.innerHTML=<div class="network-container" id="networkGraph"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="tooltip" id="tooltip"&gt;&lt;/div>;const container=document.getElementById('networkGraph');const w=container.clientWidth||800,h=600;const svg=d3.select(container).append('svg').attr('width',w).attr('height',h).style('background','var(--bg)');const link=svg.append('g').selectAll('line').data(links).enter().append('line').attr('class','link').attr('stroke','var(--border)').attr('stroke-opacity',.4);const node=svg.append('g').selectAll('g').data(nodes).enter().append('g').attr('class','node').call(d3.drag().on('start',dragstarted).on('drag',dragged).on('end',dragended));node.append('circle').attr('r',d=>d.size?d.size8:5).attr('fill',d=>{if(d.type==='function')return '#7b61ff';if(d.type==='peer')return '#ffaa44';if(d.group==='nsa')return '#2a5a7a';return '#1a2332'}).attr('stroke','var(--border)').attr('stroke-width',1.5);node.append('text').attr('class','node-label').attr('dx',d=>d.type==='function'?10:12).attr('dy',4).text(d=>d.label).style('font-size',d=>d.type==='function'?'8px':'10px').style('fill','var(--fg2)').style('text-anchor','start');const
